####################################### Dynasty: 1000048728 #######################################
1404804 = { #任得敬 Ren Dejing. First a Controller-general 通判 at Xi'an 西安州. In 1137 he surrendered to Xi Xia after Xi'an was taken by them. Made a prefect by Quanshun. In 1138 in order to curry a favour with the Emperor he introduced his daughter to the palace. In 1137 she became a concubine and he was made a Defense and Security Commissioner at Jingzhou 靜州防禦使. Due to bribery he rose in ranks at the court and became a high offical. In 1138 he was able to make his daughter an Empress, while he himself because Imperial father-in-law 上國丈爷 and he a Supreme Commander at Jingzhou 都統軍. In 1139 his daughter becomes Empress Dowager, even though the next Emperor is not her biological son. In 1140 as a reward for pacifying the rebellion of Xiao Heda 蕭合達 he is enfeoffed as Duke of Xiping 西平公 and made Supreme Commander of Xiangqing Army 翔慶軍都統軍. In 1143 he pacifies agrarian revolts in Xianzhou and Dingzhou 威州、定州等. In 1147 he conspires to have more say in the government, but is stopped by Wo Daozhong 斡道冲 and other ministers. In 1149 he is made 尚書令 中書令. In 1156 he becomes a Prime Minister 國相 after the death of Chage, his younger brothers Decong a Captain of Palace guards 殿前太尉, Degong Governor of Capital Prefecture Xingqing 興慶府尹. Soon after he forces Renzong to make him Prince of Chu 楚王. In 1165 he build a fortress in Lingzhou and a palace for himself, requests control over Shazhou, Guazhou, Lingzhou and Xiazhou. In 1170 he creates a fief for himself, Renzong is forced to consent and gives Southwestern Circuit 西南路, Xiping 西平府, Lingzhou 靈州 and other provinces to Chu. He asks for recognition from Jin, but is rebuked and instead offers a two-side attack on Jin to Song. However, his plot is discovered and Renzong with the support of Jin captures and executes Ren brothers in 8th month.
	dynasty=1000048728 #Ren

####################################### Dynasty: house_ouning_liu #######################################
chongan_jliu_013 = { #劉珙 Liu Gong, courtesy name 劉共父 Liu Gongfu, 忠肅 Zhongsu. Eldest son of Liu Ziyu. (南軒集/巻37/少傅劉公墓誌銘) In 1142 Jinshi. (八閩通志/卷49) In 1154.7.13 made 權中書舎人. (晦庵集/卷94/劉摳宻墓記) In 1156 made 主管台州崇道觀. (墓記) In 1162.9.11 made 禮部尚書. (墓記) In 1163.11.28 made 知泉州, but didn't go. (墓記) In 1164.2.24 made 知衢州. (墓記) In 1165.4.13 made 知潭州、荆湖南路安撫使. (墓記) 知潭州 until 1167.1.23. (墓記) In 1167.9.15 made 知制誥兼侍讀. (墓記) In 1167.12.22 made 同知樞密院事. (宋史/卷034) In 1168.8.7 made 兼參知政事. (宋史/卷034) 同知樞密院事兼參知政事 until 1168.9.24, on that day made 知隆興府、江南西路安撫 (宋史/卷034 and 墓記) In 1169.4.29 made 知荆南府、荆湖北路安撫使. (墓記) 知荆南府 until 1170.10.12, on that day his second mother died. (墓記) In 1171.4.11 made again 同知樞密院事, but didn't accept the post. (宋史/卷034) In 1171.6.18 made 同知樞密院事，爲荊、襄宣撫使, but didn't accept the post. (宋史/卷034) In 1172.12.17 made 知潭州、荆湖南路安撫使. (墓記) 知潭州 until 1173.4.14. (墓記) In 1175.1.25 made 知建康府、江東安撫使、行宮留守, but didn't go. (墓記) In 1178.7.17 retired. (墓記) In 1178.8.17 died. jinling_du_016 = { #杜杲 Du Gao, courtesy name 杜子昕 Du Zixin. Third son of Du Ying. (後村先生大全文集/卷150/杜郎中墓誌銘) At some point made 知濠州 [1229-1232]. (宋史/卷412) Later made 知安豐軍 [1232-1234].
